<pr_description>
Using dynamic styles with StyleX constants from defineConsts
### Describe the issue

When using a dynamic function as a style value in `stylex.create` together with a constants from a StyleX constants file (`defineConsts`), the following error occurs:

```bash
/stylex/packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/__tests__/__fixtures__/main.stylex.js: Invalid pseudo or at-rule.

      68 |       )
      69 |     ) {
    > 70 |       throw new Error(messages.INVALID_PSEUDO_OR_AT_RULE);
         |             ^
      71 |     }
      72 |     if (conditions.includes(key)) {
      73 |       throw new Error(messages.DUPLICATE_CONDITIONAL);

      at validateConditionalStyles (src/shared/preprocess-rules/basic-validation.js:70:13)
      at validateConditionalStyles (src/shared/preprocess-rules/basic-validation.js:42:9)
      at styleXCreateSet (src/shared/stylex-create.js:57:22)
      at transformStyleXCreate (src/visitors/stylex-create.js:169:19)
      at PluginPass.CallExpression (src/index.js:311:30)
      at call (../../../node_modules/@babel/traverse/src/visitors.ts:303:14)

```

### Expected behavior

Correct style transformation using constants as dynamic styles

### Steps to reproduce

Add styles as in `test case` section

### Test case

```js
// packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/__tests__/transform-stylex-defineConsts-test.js

test('dynamic styles with StyleX constants', () => {
      const { code, } = transformWithInlineConsts(`
        import * as stylex from '@stylexjs/stylex';
        import { mediaQueries } from './constants.stylex';

        export const styles = stylex.create({
          nodeEnd: (animationDuration) => ({
            transition: {
              [mediaQueries.reduceMotion]: 'none',
              default: \`transform \${animationDuration}ms ease-in-out\`,
            },
          }),
        });
      `);

      expect(code).toMatchInlineSnapshot(`
        "
          // Transformation result
        "
      `);
    });
```

### Additional comments

Thanks to @martinbooth for discovering and [reporting](https://github.com/Dwlad90/stylex-swc-plugin/issues/504) this bug

    10	import * as messages from '../messages';
    11	import { isPlainObject } from '../utils/object-utils';
    12	
    13	export function validateNamespace(
    14	  namespace: mixed,
    15	  conditions: $ReadOnlyArray<string> = [],
    16	): void {
    17	  if (!isPlainObject(namespace)) {
    18	    throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_NAMESPACE_VALUE);
    19	  }
    20	  const ns: { +[string]: mixed } = namespace;
    21	  for (const key in ns) {
    22	    const val = ns[key];
    23	    if (val === null || typeof val === 'string' || typeof val === 'number') {
    24	      continue;
    25	    }
    26	    if (Array.isArray(val)) {
    27	      for (const v of val) {
    28	        if (v === null || typeof v === 'string' || typeof v === 'number') {
    29	          continue;
    30	        }
    31	        throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_ARRAY_VALUE);
    32	      }
    33	      continue;
    34	    }
    35	    if (isPlainObject(val)) {
    36	      if (key.startsWith('@') || key.startsWith(':')) {
    37	        if (conditions.includes(key)) {
    38	          throw new Error(messages.DUPLICATE_CONDITIONAL);
    39	        }
    40	        validateNamespace(val, [...conditions, key]);
    41	      } else {
    42	        validateConditionalStyles(val as $FlowFixMe);
    43	      }
    44	      continue;
    45	    }
    46	
    47	    throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_VALUE);
    48	  }
    49	}
    50	
    51	type ConditionalStyles = $ReadOnly<{
    52	  [key: string]: string | number | ConditionalStyles,
    53	}>;
    54	
    55	function validateConditionalStyles(
    56	  val: ConditionalStyles,
    57	  conditions: $ReadOnlyArray<string> = [],
    58	): void {
    59	  for (const key in val) {
    60	    const v = val[key];
    61	    if (
    62	      !(
    63	        key.startsWith('@') ||
    64	        key.startsWith(':') ||
    65	        // This is a placeholder for `defineConsts` values that are later inlined
    66	        key.startsWith('var(--') ||
    67	        key === 'default'
    68	      )
    69	    ) {
    70	      throw new Error(messages.INVALID_PSEUDO_OR_AT_RULE);
    71	    }
    72	    if (conditions.includes(key)) {
    73	      throw new Error(messages.DUPLICATE_CONDITIONAL);
    74	    }
    75	    if (v === null || typeof v === 'string' || typeof v === 'number') {
    76	      continue;
    77	    }
    78	    if (Array.isArray(v)) {
    79	      for (const vv of v) {
    80	        if (vv === null || typeof vv === 'string' || typeof vv === 'number') {
    81	          continue;
    82	        }
    83	        throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_VALUE);
    84	      }
    85	      continue;
    86	    }
    87	    if (isPlainObject(v)) {
    88	      validateConditionalStyles(v, [...conditions, key]);
    89	      continue;
    90	    }
    91	    throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_VALUE);
    92	  }

    10	import type {
    11	  RawStyles,
    12	  InjectableStyle,
    13	  StyleXOptions,
    14	  FlatCompiledStyles,
    15	} from './common-types';
    16	import type { ComputedStyle, IPreRule } from './preprocess-rules/PreRule';
    17	
    18	import { createShortHash } from './hash';
    19	import { defaultOptions } from './utils/default-options';
    20	import { flattenRawStyleObject } from './preprocess-rules/flatten-raw-style-obj';
    21	import { validateNamespace } from './preprocess-rules/basic-validation';
    22	
    23	type TPropTuple = [+key: string, +styles: $ReadOnlyArray<ComputedStyle>];
    24	
    25	type ClassPathsInNamespace = {
    26	  +[className: string]: $ReadOnlyArray<string>,
    27	};
    28	
    29	type TClassNameTuples = $NonMaybeType<ComputedStyle>;
    30	
    31	// This takes the object of styles passed to `stylex.create` and transforms it.
    32	//   The transformation replaces style values with classNames.
    33	//
    34	// It also collects all injected styles along the way.
    35	// It then returns a tuple of the transformed style Object and an object of injected styles.
    36	//
    37	// This function does some basic validation, and then uses `styleXCreateNamespace` to transform
    38	// each namespace within,
    39	//
    40	// Before returning, it ensures that there are no duplicate styles being injected.
    41	export default function styleXCreateSet(
    42	  namespaces: { +[string]: RawStyles },
    43	  options?: StyleXOptions = defaultOptions,
    44	): [
    45	  { [string]: FlatCompiledStyles },
    46	  { [string]: InjectableStyle },
    47	  { +[string]: ClassPathsInNamespace },
    48	] {
    49	  const resolvedNamespaces: { [string]: FlatCompiledStyles } = {};
    50	  const injectedStyles: { [string]: InjectableStyle } = {};
    51	  const namespaceToClassPaths: { [string]: ClassPathsInNamespace } = {};
    52	
    53	  for (const namespaceName of Object.keys(namespaces)) {
    54	    const namespace = namespaces[namespaceName];
    55	    const classPathsInNamespace: { [string]: $ReadOnlyArray<string> } = {};
    56	
    57	    validateNamespace(namespace);
    58	
    59	    // filterReverse to remove duplicate keys and keep the last one always.
    60	    // This is the same behaviour as Object.fromEntries, except it maintains
    61	    // order correctly and is more efficient.
    62	    const seenProperties = new Set<string>();
    63	    const flattenedNamespace: $ReadOnlyArray<$ReadOnly<[string, IPreRule]>> =
    64	      flattenRawStyleObject(namespace, options).reduceRight(
    65	        (arr, curr) => {
    66	          if (seenProperties.has(curr[0])) {
    67	            return arr;
    68	          }
    69	          seenProperties.add(curr[0]);
    70	          arr.unshift(curr);
    71	          return arr;
    72	        },
    73	        [] as Array<$ReadOnly<[string, IPreRule]>>,
    74	      );
    75	
    76	    const compiledNamespaceTuples: $ReadOnlyArray<TPropTuple> =
    77	      flattenedNamespace.map(([key, value]) => {
    78	        // Skip variables-as-keys to avoid regression to dynamic styles output
    79	        if (options.enableMinifiedKeys === true && !key.startsWith('--')) {
    80	          const hashedKey = createShortHash('<>' + key);
    81	          const displayKey =
    82	            options.debug === true ? `${key}-k${hashedKey}` : `k${hashedKey}`;
    83	          return [displayKey, value.compiled(options)];
    84	        } else {
    85	          return [key, value.compiled(options)];
    86	        }
    87	      });
    88	
    89	    const namespaceObj: {
    90	      [string]: null | string,
    91	    } = {};
    92	    for (const [key, value] of compiledNamespaceTuples) {
    93	      // Remove nulls
    94	      const classNameTuples: $ReadOnlyArray<TClassNameTuples> = value
    95	        .map((v) => (Array.isArray(v) ? v : null))
    96	        .filter(Boolean);
    97	
    98	      classNameTuples.forEach(([_className, _, classesToOriginalPath]) => {
    99	        Object.assign(classPathsInNamespace, classesToOriginalPath);
   100	      });
   101	
   102	      const classNames = classNameTuples.map(([className]) => className);
   103	      const uniqueClassNames = new Set(classNames);
   104	      const className = Array.from(uniqueClassNames).join(' ');
   105	      namespaceObj[key] = className !== '' ? className : null;
   106	
   107	      for (const [className, injectable] of classNameTuples) {
   108	        if (injectedStyles[className] == null) {
   109	          injectedStyles[className] = injectable;
   110	        }
   111	      }
   112	    }
   113	    resolvedNamespaces[namespaceName] = { ...namespaceObj, $$css: true };
   114	    namespaceToClassPaths[namespaceName] = classPathsInNamespace;
   115	  }
   116	
   117	  return [resolvedNamespaces, injectedStyles, namespaceToClassPaths];
   118	}

    10	import type { NodePath } from '@babel/traverse';
    11	import type { FunctionConfig } from '../utils/evaluate-path';
    12	import type { InjectableStyle } from '../shared';
    13	
    14	import * as t from '@babel/types';
    15	import StateManager from '../utils/state-manager';
    16	import {
    17	  create as stylexCreate,
    18	  firstThatWorks as stylexFirstThatWorks,
    19	  keyframes as stylexKeyframes,
    20	  positionTry as stylexPositionTry,
    21	} from '../shared';
    22	import { addSourceMapData } from '../utils/add-sourcemap-data';
    23	import {
    24	  convertToTestStyles,
    25	  injectDevClassNames,
    26	} from '../utils/dev-classname';
    27	import {
    28	  convertObjectToAST,
    29	  removeObjectsWithSpreads,
    30	} from '../utils/js-to-ast';
    31	import { messages } from '../shared';
    32	import { evaluateStyleXCreateArg } from './parse-stylex-create-arg';
    33	import flatMapExpandedShorthands from '../shared/preprocess-rules';
    34	import { hoistExpression, pathReplaceHoisted } from '../utils/ast-helpers';
    35	
    36	function isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr: t.Expression): boolean {
    37	  if (t.isTemplateLiteral(expr)) return true;
    38	
    39	  if (
    40	    t.isStringLiteral(expr) ||
    41	    t.isNumericLiteral(expr) ||
    42	    t.isBooleanLiteral(expr)
    43	  )
    44	    return true;
    45	
    46	  if (t.isBinaryExpression(expr)) {
    47	    return ['+', '-', '*', '/', '%', '**'].includes(expr.operator);
    48	  }
    49	
    50	  if (t.isUnaryExpression(expr)) {
    51	    return ['-', '+'].includes(expr.operator);
    52	  }
    53	
    54	  if (t.isConditionalExpression(expr)) {
    55	    return (
    56	      isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.consequent) &&
    57	      isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.alternate)
    58	    );
    59	  }
    60	
    61	  if (t.isLogicalExpression(expr)) {
    62	    if (expr.operator === '??' || expr.operator === '||') {
    63	      return (
    64	        isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.left) || isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.right)
    65	      );
    66	    }
    67	    if (expr.operator === '&&') {
    68	      return (
    69	        isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.left) && isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr.right)
    70	      );
    71	    }
    72	  }
    73	
    74	  return false;
    75	}
    76	
    77	/// This function looks for `stylex.create` calls and transforms them.
    78	/// 1. It finds the first argument to `stylex.create` and validates it.
    79	/// 2. It pre-processes valid-dynamic parts of style object such as custom presets (spreads)
    80	/// 3. It evaluates the style object to get a JS object. This also handles local constants automatically.
    81	/// 4. It uses the `stylexCreate` from `@stylexjs/shared` to transform the JS
    82	///    object and to get a list of injected styles.
    83	/// 5. It converts the resulting Object back into an AST and replaces the call with it.
    84	/// 6. It also inserts `stylex.inject` calls above the current statement as needed.
    85	export default function transformStyleXCreate(
    86	  path: NodePath<t.CallExpression>,
    87	  state: StateManager,
    88	) {
    89	  const { node } = path;
    90	
    91	  if (node.type !== 'CallExpression') {
    92	    return;
    93	  }
    94	
    95	  if (
    96	    (node.callee.type === 'Identifier' &&
    97	      state.stylexCreateImport.has(node.callee.name)) ||
    98	    (node.callee.type === 'MemberExpression' &&
    99	      node.callee.object.type === 'Identifier' &&
   100	      node.callee.property.type === 'Identifier' &&
   101	      node.callee.property.name === 'create' &&
   102	      state.stylexImport.has(node.callee.object.name))
   103	  ) {
   104	    validateStyleXCreate(path);
   105	
   106	    const args: $ReadOnlyArray<
   107	      NodePath<
   108	        | t.Expression
   109	        | t.SpreadElement
   110	        | t.JSXNamespacedName
   111	        | t.ArgumentPlaceholder,
   112	      >,
   113	    > = path.get('arguments');
   114	    const firstArg = args[0];
   115	
   116	    state.inStyleXCreate = true;
   117	
   118	    const otherInjectedCSSRules: { [propertyName: string]: InjectableStyle } =
   119	      {};
   120	
   121	    // eslint-disable-next-line no-inner-declarations
   122	    function keyframes<
   123	      Obj: {
   124	        +[key: string]: { +[k: string]: string | number },
   125	      },
   126	    >(animation: Obj): string {
   127	      const [animationName, injectedStyle] = stylexKeyframes(
   128	        animation,
   129	        state.options,
   130	      );
   131	      otherInjectedCSSRules[animationName] = injectedStyle;
   132	      return animationName;
   133	    }
   134	
   135	    // eslint-disable-next-line no-inner-declarations
   136	    function positionTry<
   137	      Obj: {
   138	        +[k: string]: string | number,
   139	      },
   140	    >(fallbackStyles: Obj): string {
   141	      const [positionTryName, injectedStyle] = stylexPositionTry(
   142	        fallbackStyles,
   143	        state.options,
   144	      );
   145	      otherInjectedCSSRules[positionTryName] = injectedStyle;
   146	      return positionTryName;
   147	    }
   148	
   149	    const identifiers: FunctionConfig['identifiers'] = {};
   150	    const memberExpressions: FunctionConfig['memberExpressions'] = {};
   151	    state.stylexFirstThatWorksImport.forEach((name) => {
   152	      identifiers[name] = { fn: stylexFirstThatWorks };
   153	    });
   154	    state.stylexKeyframesImport.forEach((name) => {
   155	      identifiers[name] = { fn: keyframes };
   156	    });
   157	    state.stylexPositionTryImport.forEach((name) => {
   158	      identifiers[name] = { fn: positionTry };
   159	    });
   160	    state.stylexImport.forEach((name) => {
   161	      if (memberExpressions[name] == null) {
   162	        memberExpressions[name] = {};
   163	      }
   164	      memberExpressions[name].firstThatWorks = { fn: stylexFirstThatWorks };
   165	      memberExpressions[name].keyframes = { fn: keyframes };
   166	      memberExpressions[name].positionTry = { fn: positionTry };
   167	    });
   168	
   169	    const { confident, value, fns, reason, deopt } = evaluateStyleXCreateArg(
   170	      firstArg,
   171	      state,
   172	      {
   173	        identifiers,
   174	        memberExpressions,
   175	      },
   176	    );
   177	
   178	    if (!confident) {
   179	      throw (deopt ?? path).buildCodeFrameError(
   180	        reason ?? messages.nonStaticValue('create'),
   181	        SyntaxError,
   182	      );
   183	    }
   184	    const plainObject = value;
   185	
   186	    // add injection that mark variables used for dynamic styles as `inherits: false`
   187	    const injectedInheritStyles: { [string]: InjectableStyle } = {};
   188	    if (fns != null) {
   189	      const dynamicFnsNames = Object.values(fns)
   190	        ?.map((entry) =>
   191	          Object.entries(entry[1]).map(([variableName, obj]) => ({
   192	            variableName,
   193	            path: obj.path,
   194	          })),
   195	        )
   196	        .flat();
   197	
   198	      dynamicFnsNames.forEach(({ variableName, path }) => {
   199	        // Pseudo elements can only access css vars via inheritance
   200	        const isPseudoElement = path.some((p) => p.startsWith('::'));
   201	        injectedInheritStyles[variableName] = {
   202	          priority: 0,
   203	          ltr: `@property ${variableName} { syntax: "*";${isPseudoElement ? '' : ' inherits: false;'}}`,
   204	          rtl: null,
   205	        };
   206	      });
   207	    }
   208	
   209	    // eslint-disable-next-line prefer-const
   210	    let [compiledStyles, injectedStylesSansKeyframes, classPathsPerNamespace] =
   211	      stylexCreate(plainObject, state.options);
   212	
   213	    const injectedStyles = {
   214	      ...otherInjectedCSSRules,
   215	      ...injectedStylesSansKeyframes,
   216	      ...injectedInheritStyles,
   217	    };
   218	
   219	    let varName = null;
   220	    if (path.parentPath.isVariableDeclarator()) {
   221	      const idNode = path.parentPath.node.id;
   222	      if (idNode.type === 'Identifier') {
   223	        varName = idNode.name;
   224	      }
   225	    }
   226	
   227	    if (state.isDebug && state.opts.enableDebugDataProp) {
   228	      compiledStyles = {
   229	        ...addSourceMapData(compiledStyles, path, state),
   230	      };
   231	    }
   232	    if (state.isDev && state.opts.enableDevClassNames) {
   233	      compiledStyles = {
   234	        ...injectDevClassNames(compiledStyles, varName, state),
   235	      };
   236	    }
   237	    if (state.isTest) {
   238	      compiledStyles = {
   239	        ...convertToTestStyles(compiledStyles, varName, state),
   240	      };
   241	    }
   242	
   243	    if (varName != null) {
   244	      const stylesToRemember = removeObjectsWithSpreads(compiledStyles);
   245	      state.styleMap.set(varName, stylesToRemember);
   246	      state.styleVars.set(varName, path.parentPath as $FlowFixMe);
   247	    }
   248	
   249	    const resultAst = convertObjectToAST(compiledStyles);
   250	
   251	    if (fns != null) {
   252	      resultAst.properties = resultAst.properties.map((prop) => {
   253	        if (t.isObjectProperty(prop)) {
   254	          const key =
   255	            prop.key.type === 'Identifier' && !prop.computed
   256	              ? prop.key.name
   257	              : prop.key.type === 'StringLiteral'
   258	                ? prop.key.value
   259	                : null;
   260	          if (key != null && Object.keys(fns).includes(key)) {
   261	            const [params, inlineStyles] = fns[key];
   262	
   263	            const origClassPaths: { [string]: string } = {};
   264	
   265	            for (const [className, classPaths] of Object.entries(
   266	              classPathsPerNamespace[key],
   267	            )) {
   268	              origClassPaths[className] = classPaths.join('_');
   269	            }
   270	
   271	            let dynamicStyles: $ReadOnlyArray<{
   272	              +expression: t.Expression,
   273	              +key: string,
   274	              path: string,
   275	            }> = Object.entries(inlineStyles).map(([_key, v]) => ({
   276	              expression: v.originalExpression,
   277	              key: v.path
   278	                .slice(
   279	                  0,
   280	                  v.path.findIndex(
   281	                    (p) => !p.startsWith(':') && !p.startsWith('@'),
   282	                  ) + 1,
   283	                )
   284	                .join('_'),
   285	              path: v.path.join('_'),
   286	            }));
   287	
   288	            if (state.options.styleResolution === 'legacy-expand-shorthands') {
   289	              dynamicStyles = legacyExpandShorthands(dynamicStyles);
   290	            }
   291	
   292	            if (t.isObjectExpression(prop.value)) {
   293	              const value: t.ObjectExpression = prop.value;
   294	
   295	              let cssTagValue: t.Expression | t.PatternLike =
   296	                t.booleanLiteral(true);
   297	
   298	              const staticProps: Array<t.ObjectProperty> = [];
   299	
   300	              const conditionalProps: Array<t.ObjectProperty> = [];
   301	
   302	              value.properties.forEach((prop) => {
   303	                if (!t.isObjectProperty(prop) || t.isPrivateName(prop.key)) {
   304	                  return;
   305	                }
   306	
   307	                const objProp: t.ObjectProperty = prop;
   308	                const propKey =
   309	                  t.isIdentifier(objProp.key) && !objProp.computed
   310	                    ? objProp.key.name
   311	                    : t.isStringLiteral(objProp.key)
   312	                      ? objProp.key.value
   313	                      : null;
   314	
   315	                if (propKey == null) {
   316	                  staticProps.push(objProp);
   317	                  return;
   318	                }
   319	
   320	                if (propKey === '$$css') {
   321	                  cssTagValue = objProp.value;
   322	                  return;
   323	                }
   324	
   325	                const classList = t.isStringLiteral(objProp.value)
   326	                  ? objProp.value.value.split(' ')
   327	                  : [];
   328	
   329	                let isStatic = true;
   330	                const exprList: t.Expression[] = [];
   331	
   332	                classList.forEach((cls, index) => {
   333	                  const expr = dynamicStyles.find(
   334	                    ({ path }) => origClassPaths[cls] === path,
   335	                  )?.expression;
   336	
   337	                  const isLast = index === classList.length - 1;
   338	                  const clsWithSpace = isLast ? cls : cls + ' ';
   339	
   340	                  if (expr && !isSafeToSkipNullCheck(expr)) {
   341	                    isStatic = false;
   342	                    exprList.push(
   343	                      t.conditionalExpression(
   344	                        t.binaryExpression('!=', expr, t.nullLiteral()),
   345	                        t.stringLiteral(clsWithSpace),
   346	                        expr,
   347	                      ),
   348	                    );
   349	                  } else {
   350	                    exprList.push(t.stringLiteral(clsWithSpace));
   351	                  }
   352	                });
   353	
   354	                const joined =
   355	                  exprList.length === 0
   356	                    ? t.stringLiteral('')
   357	                    : exprList.reduce((acc, curr) =>
   358	                        t.binaryExpression('+', acc, curr),
   359	                      );
   360	
   361	                if (isStatic) {
   362	                  staticProps.push(t.objectProperty(objProp.key, joined));
   363	                } else {
   364	                  conditionalProps.push(t.objectProperty(objProp.key, joined));
   365	                }
   366	              });
   367	
   368	              let staticObj = null;
   369	              let conditionalObj = null;
   370	
   371	              if (staticProps.length > 0) {
   372	                staticProps.push(
   373	                  t.objectProperty(t.stringLiteral('$$css'), cssTagValue),
   374	                );
   375	                staticObj = t.objectExpression(staticProps);
   376	              }
   377	
   378	              if (conditionalProps.length > 0) {
   379	                conditionalProps.push(
   380	                  t.objectProperty(t.identifier('$$css'), cssTagValue),
   381	                );
   382	                conditionalObj = t.objectExpression(conditionalProps);
   383	              }
   384	
   385	              let finalFnValue: t.Expression = t.objectExpression(
   386	                Object.entries(inlineStyles).map(([key, val]) =>
   387	                  t.objectProperty(t.stringLiteral(key), val.expression),
   388	                ),
   389	              );
   390	              if (staticObj != null || conditionalObj != null) {
   391	                finalFnValue = t.arrayExpression(
   392	                  [
   393	                    staticObj && hoistExpression(path, staticObj),
   394	                    conditionalObj,
   395	                    finalFnValue,
   396	                  ].filter(Boolean),
   397	                );
   398	              }
   399	
   400	              prop.value = t.arrowFunctionExpression(params, finalFnValue);
   401	            }
   402	          }
   403	        }
   404	
   405	        return prop;
   406	      });
   407	    }
   408	
   409	    const listOfStyles = Object.entries(injectedStyles).map(
   410	      ([key, { priority, ...rest }]) => [key, rest, priority],
   411	    );
   412	
   413	    state.registerStyles(listOfStyles, path);
   414	
   415	    pathReplaceHoisted(path, resultAst);
   416	
   417	    if (Object.keys(injectedStyles).length === 0) {
   418	      return;
   419	    }
   420	  }
   421	  state.inStyleXCreate = false;
   422	}
   423	
   424	// Validates the first argument to `stylex.create`.
   425	function validateStyleXCreate(path: NodePath<t.CallExpression>) {
   426	  if (path.parentPath == null || path.parentPath.isExpressionStatement()) {
   427	    throw path.buildCodeFrameError(
   428	      messages.unboundCallValue('create'),
   429	      SyntaxError,
   430	    );
   431	  }
   432	
   433	  if (path.node.arguments.length !== 1) {
   434	    throw path.buildCodeFrameError(
   435	      messages.illegalArgumentLength('create', 1),
   436	      SyntaxError,
   437	    );
   438	  }
   439	
   440	  const arg = path.node.arguments[0];
   441	  if (arg.type !== 'ObjectExpression') {
   442	    throw path.buildCodeFrameError(
   443	      messages.nonStyleObject('create'),
   444	      SyntaxError,
   445	    );
   446	  }
   447	
   448	  const hasSpread = arg.properties.some((prop) => t.isSpreadElement(prop));
   449	  if (hasSpread) {
   450	    throw path.buildCodeFrameError(messages.NO_OBJECT_SPREADS, SyntaxError);
   451	  }
   452	}
   453	
   454	function legacyExpandShorthands(
   455	  dynamicStyles: $ReadOnlyArray<{
   456	    +expression: t.Expression,
   457	    +key: string,
   458	    path: string,
   459	  }>,
   460	): $ReadOnlyArray<{
   461	  +expression: t.Expression,
   462	  +key: string,
   463	  path: string,
   464	}> {
   465	  const expandedKeysToKeyPaths = dynamicStyles
   466	    .flatMap(({ key }, i) => {
   467	      return flatMapExpandedShorthands([key, 'p' + i], {
   468	        styleResolution: 'legacy-expand-shorthands',
   469	      });
   470	    })
   471	    .map(([key, value]) => {
   472	      if (typeof value !== 'string') {
   473	        return null;
   474	      }
   475	      const index = parseInt(value.slice(1), 10);
   476	      const thatDynStyle = dynamicStyles[index];
   477	      return {
   478	        ...thatDynStyle,
   479	        key,
   480	        path:
   481	          thatDynStyle.path === thatDynStyle.key
   482	            ? key
   483	            : thatDynStyle.path.includes(thatDynStyle.key + '_')
   484	              ? thatDynStyle.path.replace(thatDynStyle.key + '_', key + '_')
   485	              : thatDynStyle.path.replace('_' + thatDynStyle.key, '_' + key),
   486	      };
   487	    })
   488	    .filter(Boolean);
   489	
   490	  return expandedKeysToKeyPaths;
   491	}
   492

    55	function validateConditionalStyles(
    56	  val: ConditionalStyles,
    57	  conditions: $ReadOnlyArray<string> = [],
    58	): void {
    59	  for (const key in val) {
    60	    const v = val[key];
    61	    if (
    62	      !(
    63	        key.startsWith('@') ||
    64	        key.startsWith(':') ||
    65	        // This is a placeholder for `defineConsts` values that are later inlined
    66	        key.startsWith('var(--') ||
    67	        key === 'default'
    68	      )
    69	    ) {
    70	      throw new Error(messages.INVALID_PSEUDO_OR_AT_RULE);
    71	    }
    72	    if (conditions.includes(key)) {
    73	      throw new Error(messages.DUPLICATE_CONDITIONAL);
    74	    }
    75	    if (v === null || typeof v === 'string' || typeof v === 'number') {
    76	      continue;
    77	    }
    78	    if (Array.isArray(v)) {
    79	      for (const vv of v) {
    80	        if (vv === null || typeof vv === 'string' || typeof vv === 'number') {
    81	          continue;
    82	        }
    83	        throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_VALUE);
    84	      }
    85	      continue;
    86	    }
    87	    if (isPlainObject(v)) {
    88	      validateConditionalStyles(v, [...conditions, key]);
    89	      continue;
    90	    }
    91	    throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_VALUE);

Now I understand the issue. The problem is in the `validateConditionalStyles` function. When using dynamic styles with constants from `defineConsts`, the constants need to be properly handled. The validation logic doesn't recognize constants as valid keys for conditional styles.

Looking at the code, I can see that the validation expects conditional style keys to:
1. Start with `@` (for media queries)
2. Start with `:` (for pseudo classes/elements) 
3. Start with `var(--` (for CSS variables)
4. Be `default`

However, when using constants from `defineConsts`, these constants might contain media queries like `@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)`, but during validation, they are treated as regular string values rather than media queries.

Let me examine how constants are processed and inline their values:

     1	/**
     2	 * Copyright (c) Meta Platforms, Inc. and affiliates.
     3	 *
     4	 * This source code is licensed under the MIT license found in the
     5	 * LICENSE file in the root directory of this source tree.
     6	 *
     7	 * @flow strict
     8	 */
     9	
    10	import type { NodePath } from '@babel/traverse';
    11	
    12	import * as t from '@babel/types';
    13	import { evaluate } from '../utils/evaluate-path';
    14	import { utils, defineConsts as styleXDefineConsts, messages } from '../shared';
    15	import { convertObjectToAST } from '../utils/js-to-ast';
    16	import StateManager from '../utils/state-manager';
    17	
    18	/// This function looks for `stylex.defineConsts` calls and transforms them.
    19	/// 1. It finds and validates the first argument to `stylex.defineConsts`.
    20	/// 2. It evaluates the style const object to a JS value, erroring on non-static or non-object values.
    21	/// 3. It generates a theme name from the filename and export name for hashing.
    22	/// 4. It invokes `stylexDefineConsts` to transform the JS object and collect injected styles.
    23	/// 5. It creates a map of key-value pairs of constants to be inlined.
    24	/// 6. It replaces the call with the transformed AST and registers the styles in state.
    25	export default function transformStyleXDefineConsts(
    26	  callExpressionPath: NodePath<t.CallExpression>,
    27	  state: StateManager,
    28	) {
    29	  const callExpressionNode = callExpressionPath.node;
    30	  if (callExpressionNode.type !== 'CallExpression') return;
    31	
    32	  if (
    33	    (callExpressionNode.callee.type === 'Identifier' &&
    34	      state.stylexDefineConstsImport.has(callExpressionNode.callee.name)) ||
    35	    (callExpressionNode.callee.type === 'MemberExpression' &&
    36	      callExpressionNode.callee.property.name === 'defineConsts' &&
    37	      callExpressionNode.callee.object.type === 'Identifier' &&
    38	      state.stylexImport.has(callExpressionNode.callee.object.name))
    39	  ) {
    40	    validateStyleXDefineConsts(callExpressionPath);
    41	
    42	    const variableDeclaratorPath = callExpressionPath.parentPath;
    43	    if (!variableDeclaratorPath.isVariableDeclarator()) return;
    44	
    45	    const variableDeclaratorNode = variableDeclaratorPath.node;
    46	    if (variableDeclaratorNode.id.type !== 'Identifier') return;
    47	
    48	    const varId: t.Identifier = variableDeclaratorNode.id;
    49	    const args = callExpressionPath.get('arguments');
    50	    const firstArg = args[0];
    51	
    52	    const { confident, value } = evaluate(firstArg, state);
    53	    if (!confident) {
    54	      throw callExpressionPath.buildCodeFrameError(
    55	        messages.nonStaticValue('defineConsts'),
    56	        SyntaxError,
    57	      );
    58	    }
    59	    if (typeof value !== 'object' || value == null) {
    60	      throw callExpressionPath.buildCodeFrameError(
    61	        messages.nonStyleObject('defineConsts'),
    62	        SyntaxError,
    63	      );
    64	    }
    65	
    66	    const fileName = state.fileNameForHashing;
    67	    if (fileName == null) {
    68	      throw new Error(messages.cannotGenerateHash('defineConsts'));
    69	    }
    70	
    71	    const exportName = varId.name;
    72	    const exportId = utils.genFileBasedIdentifier({ fileName, exportName });
    73	
    74	    const [transformedJsOutput, jsOutput] = styleXDefineConsts(value, {
    75	      ...state.options,
    76	      exportId,
    77	    });
    78	
    79	    callExpressionPath.replaceWith(convertObjectToAST(transformedJsOutput));
    80	
    81	    const styles = Object.entries(jsOutput).map(([_, obj]) => [
    82	      obj.constKey,
    83	      {
    84	        constKey: obj.constKey,
    85	        constVal: obj.constVal,
    86	        ltr: obj.ltr,
    87	        rtl: obj.rtl ?? null,
    88	      },
    89	      obj.priority,
    90	    ]);
    91	
    92	    state.registerStyles(styles);
    93	  }
    94	}
    95	
    96	function validateStyleXDefineConsts(
    97	  callExpressionPath: NodePath<t.CallExpression>,
    98	) {
    99	  const variableDeclaratorPath = callExpressionPath.parentPath;
   100	  const exportNamedDeclarationPath =
   101	    variableDeclaratorPath.parentPath?.parentPath;
   102	
   103	  if (
   104	    variableDeclaratorPath == null ||
   105	    !variableDeclaratorPath.isVariableDeclarator() ||
   106	    variableDeclaratorPath.node.id.type !== 'Identifier'
   107	  ) {
   108	    throw callExpressionPath.buildCodeFrameError(
   109	      messages.unboundCallValue('defineConsts'),
   110	      SyntaxError,
   111	    );
   112	  }
   113	
   114	  if (
   115	    exportNamedDeclarationPath == null ||
   116	    !exportNamedDeclarationPath.isExportNamedDeclaration()
   117	  ) {
   118	    throw callExpressionPath.buildCodeFrameError(
   119	      messages.nonExportNamedDeclaration('defineConsts'),
   120	      SyntaxError,
   121	    );
   122	  }
   123	
   124	  if (callExpressionPath.node.arguments.length !== 1) {
   125	    throw callExpressionPath.buildCodeFrameError(
   126	      messages.illegalArgumentLength('defineConsts', 1),
   127	      SyntaxError,
   128	    );
   129	  }
   130	}
   131

    10	import type { InjectableConstStyle, StyleXOptions } from './common-types';
    11	import type { ConstsConfig } from './stylex-consts-utils';
    12	
    13	import { defaultOptions } from './utils/default-options';
    14	import * as messages from './messages';
    15	
    16	import createHash from './hash';
    17	
    18	export default function styleXDefineConsts<Vars: ConstsConfig>(
    19	  constants: Vars,
    20	  options: $ReadOnly<{ ...Partial<StyleXOptions>, exportId: string, ... }>,
    21	): [
    22	  { [string]: string | number }, // jsOutput JS output
    23	  { [string]: InjectableConstStyle }, // metadata for registerinjectableStyles
    24	] {
    25	  const { classNamePrefix, exportId, debug, enableDebugClassNames } = {
    26	    ...defaultOptions,
    27	    ...options,
    28	  };
    29	
    30	  const jsOutput: { [string]: string | number } = {};
    31	  const injectableStyles: { [string]: InjectableConstStyle } = {};
    32	
    33	  for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(constants)) {
    34	    if (key.startsWith('--')) {
    35	      throw new Error(messages.INVALID_CONST_KEY);
    36	    }
    37	
    38	    const varSafeKey = (
    39	      key[0] >= '0' && key[0] <= '9' ? `_${key}` : key
    40	    ).replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9]/g, '_');
    41	
    42	    const constKey =
    43	      debug && enableDebugClassNames
    44	        ? `${varSafeKey}-${classNamePrefix}${createHash(`${exportId}.${key}`)}`
    45	        : `${classNamePrefix}${createHash(`${exportId}.${key}`)}`;
    46	
    47	    jsOutput[key] = value;
    48	    injectableStyles[constKey] = {
    49	      constKey,
    50	      constVal: value,
    51	      priority: 0,
    52	      ltr: '',
    53	      rtl: null,
    54	    };
    55	  }
    56	
    57	  return [jsOutput, injectableStyles];
    58	}

Now I need to understand how the constants are processed when they're used in `stylex.create`. The issue seems to be that when constants are used as keys in conditional styles, they are not properly recognized during validation.

Let me check how the constants get inlined during the transformation process. The key insight is that the validation needs to understand that constants from `defineConsts` can contain values that should be treated as valid conditional keys (like media queries).

     1	/**
     2	 * Copyright (c) Meta Platforms, Inc. and affiliates.
     3	 *
     4	 * This source code is licensed under the MIT license found in the
     5	 * LICENSE file in the root directory of this source tree.
     6	 *
     7	 * @flow strict

    10	/* eslint-disable no-unused-vars */
    11	import type { NodePath } from '@babel/traverse';
    12	import type { FunctionConfig } from '../utils/evaluate-path';
    13	
    14	import * as t from '@babel/types';
    15	import StateManager from '../utils/state-manager';
    16	import { evaluate } from '../utils/evaluate-path';
    17	import { create, utils } from '../shared';
    18	import { messages } from '../shared';
    19	import {
    20	  timeUnits,
    21	  lengthUnits,
    22	  getNumberSuffix,
    23	} from '../shared/utils/transform-value';
    24	
    25	type TInlineStyles = {
    26	  [string]: {
    27	    +path: $ReadOnlyArray<string>,
    28	    +originalExpression: t.Expression,
    29	    +expression: t.Expression | t.PatternLike,
    30	  },
    31	};
    32	
    33	type DynamicFns = {
    34	  [string]: [
    35	    +params: Array<t.Identifier>,
    36	    +inlineStyles: $ReadOnly<TInlineStyles>,
    37	  ],
    38	};
    39	
    40	// This
    41	export function evaluateStyleXCreateArg(
    42	  path: NodePath<>,
    43	  traversalState: StateManager,
    44	  functions: FunctionConfig = { identifiers: {}, memberExpressions: {} },
    45	): $ReadOnly<{
    46	  confident: boolean,
    47	  value: any,
    48	  deopt?: null | NodePath<>,
    49	  reason?: string,
    50	  fns?: DynamicFns,
    51	}> {
    52	  if (!path.isObjectExpression()) {
    53	    return evaluate(path, traversalState, functions);
    54	  }
    55	
    56	  const value: { [string]: mixed } = {};
    57	  const fns: DynamicFns = {};
    58	
    59	  for (const prop of path.get('properties')) {
    60	    if (!prop.isObjectProperty()) {
    61	      return evaluate(path, traversalState, functions);
    62	    }
    63	    const objPropPath: NodePath<t.ObjectProperty> = prop;
    64	    const keyResult = evaluateObjKey(objPropPath, traversalState, functions);
    65	    if (!keyResult.confident) {
    66	      return { confident: false, deopt: keyResult.deopt, value: null };
    67	    }
    68	    const key = keyResult.value;
    69	
    70	    const valPath = prop.get('value');
    71	    if (!valPath.isArrowFunctionExpression()) {
    72	      const val = evaluate(valPath, traversalState, functions);
    73	      if (!val.confident) {
    74	        return val;
    75	      }
    76	      value[key] = val.value;
    77	      continue;
    78	    }
    79	    const fnPath: NodePath<t.ArrowFunctionExpression> = valPath;
    80	    const allParams: Array<
    81	      NodePath<t.Identifier | t.SpreadElement | t.Pattern>,
    82	    > = fnPath.get('params');
    83	
    84	    validateDynamicStyleParams(fnPath, allParams);
    85	
    86	    const params: Array<t.Identifier> = allParams
    87	      .filter(
    88	        (
    89	          param: NodePath<t.Identifier | t.Pattern | t.SpreadElement>,
    90	        ): param is NodePath<t.Identifier> => param.isIdentifier(),
    91	      )
    92	      .map((param) => param.node);
    93	
    94	    const fnBody = fnPath.get('body');
    95	    if (!fnBody.isObjectExpression()) {
    96	      // We only allow arrow functions without block bodies.
    97	      return evaluate(path, traversalState, functions);
    98	    }
    99	    const fnObjectBody: NodePath<t.ObjectExpression> = fnBody;
   100	    const evalResult = evaluatePartialObjectRecursively(
   101	      fnObjectBody,
   102	      traversalState,
   103	      functions,
   104	    );
   105	
   106	    if (!evalResult.confident) {
   107	      const { confident, value: v, deopt } = evalResult;
   108	      return { confident, value: v, deopt };
   109	    }
   110	    const { value: v, inlineStyles } = evalResult;
   111	    value[key] = v;
   112	    fns[key] = [params, inlineStyles ?? {}];
   113	  }
   114	
   115	  return { value, confident: true, fns };
   116	}
   117	
   118	function evaluatePartialObjectRecursively(
   119	  path: NodePath<t.ObjectExpression>,
   120	  traversalState: StateManager,
   121	  functions: FunctionConfig = { identifiers: {}, memberExpressions: {} },
   122	  keyPath: $ReadOnlyArray<string> = [],
   123	): $ReadOnly<{
   124	  confident: boolean,
   125	  value: any,
   126	  deopt?: null | NodePath<>,
   127	  reason?: string,
   128	  inlineStyles?: $ReadOnly<TInlineStyles>,
   129	}> {
   130	  const obj: { [string]: mixed } = {};
   131	  const inlineStyles: TInlineStyles = {};
   132	  const props: $ReadOnlyArray<
   133	    NodePath<t.ObjectMethod | t.ObjectProperty | t.SpreadElement>,
   134	  > = path.get('properties');
   135	  for (const prop of props) {
   136	    if (prop.isObjectMethod()) {
   137	      return { value: null, confident: false };
   138	    }
   139	    if (prop.isSpreadElement()) {
   140	      const result = evaluate(prop.get('argument'), traversalState, functions);
   141	      if (!result.confident) {
   142	        return result;
   143	      }
   144	      Object.assign(obj, result.value);
   145	      continue;
   146	    }
   147	    if (prop.isObjectProperty()) {
   148	      const keyResult = evaluateObjKey(prop, traversalState, functions);
   149	      if (!keyResult.confident) {
   150	        return { confident: false, deopt: keyResult.deopt, value: null };
   151	      }
   152	      let key = keyResult.value;
   153	      if (key.startsWith('var(') && key.endsWith(')')) {
   154	        key = key.slice(4, -1);
   155	      }
   156	
   157	      const valuePath: NodePath<t.Expression | t.PatternLike> =
   158	        prop.get('value');
   159	
   160	      if (valuePath.isObjectExpression()) {
   161	        const result = evaluatePartialObjectRecursively(
   162	          valuePath,
   163	          traversalState,
   164	          functions,
   165	          [...keyPath, key],
   166	        );
   167	        if (!result.confident) {
   168	          return { confident: false, deopt: result.deopt, value: null };
   169	        }
   170	        obj[key] = result.value;
   171	        Object.assign(inlineStyles, result.inlineStyles);
   172	      } else {
   173	        const result = evaluate(valuePath, traversalState, functions);
   174	        if (!result.confident) {
   175	          const fullKeyPath = [...keyPath, key];
   176	          const varName =
   177	            '--x-' +
   178	            (keyPath.length > 0
   179	              ? utils.hash([...keyPath, key].join('_'))
   180	              : key);
   181	          obj[key] = `var(${varName})`;
   182	          const node = valuePath.node;
   183	          if (!t.isExpression(node)) {
   184	            throw valuePath.buildCodeFrameError(
   185	              'Expected expression as style value',
   186	              SyntaxError,
   187	            );
   188	          }
   189	          const expression: t.Expression = node as $FlowFixMe;
   190	
   191	          const propName =
   192	            fullKeyPath.find(
   193	              (k) =>
   194	                !k.startsWith(':') && !k.startsWith('@') && k !== 'default',
   195	            ) ?? key;
   196	
   197	          const unit =
   198	            timeUnits.has(propName) || lengthUnits.has(propName)
   199	              ? getNumberSuffix(propName)
   200	              : '';
   201	
   202	          const inlineStyleExpression =
   203	            unit !== ''
   204	              ? t.callExpression(
   205	                  t.arrowFunctionExpression(
   206	                    [t.identifier('val')],
   207	                    t.conditionalExpression(
   208	                      t.binaryExpression(
   209	                        '===',
   210	                        t.unaryExpression('typeof', t.identifier('val')),
   211	                        t.stringLiteral('number'),
   212	                      ),
   213	                      t.binaryExpression(
   214	                        '+',
   215	                        t.identifier('val'),
   216	                        t.stringLiteral(unit),
   217	                      ),
   218	                      t.conditionalExpression(
   219	                        t.binaryExpression(
   220	                          '!=',
   221	                          t.identifier('val'),
   222	                          t.nullLiteral(),
   223	                        ),
   224	                        t.identifier('val'),
   225	                        t.identifier('undefined'),
   226	                      ),
   227	                    ),
   228	                  ),
   229	                  [expression as t.Expression],
   230	                )
   231	              : t.conditionalExpression(
   232	                  t.binaryExpression('!=', expression, t.nullLiteral()),
   233	                  expression,
   234	                  t.identifier('undefined'),
   235	                );
   236	          inlineStyles[varName] = {
   237	            path: [...keyPath, key],
   238	            originalExpression: expression,
   239	            expression: inlineStyleExpression,
   240	          };
   241	        } else {
   242	          obj[key] = result.value;
   243	        }
   244	      }
   245	    }
   246	  }
   247	  return { value: obj, confident: true, inlineStyles };
   248	}
   249	
   250	type KeyResult =
   251	  | { confident: true, value: string }
   252	  | { confident: false, deopt?: null | NodePath<> };
   253	
   254	function evaluateObjKey(
   255	  prop: NodePath<t.ObjectProperty>,
   256	  traversalState: StateManager,
   257	  functions: FunctionConfig,
   258	): KeyResult {
   259	  const keyPath: NodePath<t.ObjectProperty['key']> = prop.get('key');
   260	  let key: string;
   261	  if ((prop.node as t.ObjectProperty).computed) {
   262	    const result = evaluate(keyPath, traversalState, functions);
   263	    if (!result.confident) {
   264	      return { confident: false, deopt: result.deopt };
   265	    }
   266	    key = result.value;
   267	  } else if (keyPath.isIdentifier()) {
   268	    key = keyPath.node.name;
   269	  } else {
   270	    // TODO: This is'nt handling all possible types that `keyPath` could be
   271	    key = (keyPath.node as $FlowFixMe).value;
   272	  }
   273	  return {
   274	    confident: true,
   275	    value: String(key),
   276	  };
   277	}
   278	
   279	function validateDynamicStyleParams(
   280	  path: NodePath<t.ArrowFunctionExpression>,
   281	  params: Array<NodePath<t.Identifier | t.SpreadElement | t.Pattern>>,
   282	) {
   283	  if (params.some((param) => !param.isIdentifier())) {
   284	    throw path.buildCodeFrameError(
   285	      messages.ONLY_NAMED_PARAMETERS_IN_DYNAMIC_STYLE_FUNCTIONS,
   286	      SyntaxError,
   287	    );
   288	  }
   289	}
   290

2026-01-09 01:43:03,301 - INFO - swea-agent - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I understand the issue. Let me trace through what's happening:

1. When we have a dynamic function with constants from `defineConsts`, the computed property keys get evaluated in `evaluateObjKey` function.
2. When the key is a constant from `defineConsts` (like `mediaQueries.reduceMotion`), it evaluates to something like `"var(--x-...)"` (a CSS variable placeholder).
3. This placeholder string is then passed to `validateConditionalStyles`.
4. The validation function checks if the key starts with `@`, `:`, `var(--`, or is `'default'`.

Looking at the validation logic in `/testbed/packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/src/shared/preprocess-rules/basic-validation.js`, I can see that the issue is that `defineConsts` constants get converted to CSS variable placeholders, but the validation doesn't recognize them properly.

Let me analyze the specific issue:

   251	  | { confident: true, value: string }
   252	  | { confident: false, deopt?: null | NodePath<> };
   253	
   254	function evaluateObjKey(
   255	  prop: NodePath<t.ObjectProperty>,
   256	  traversalState: StateManager,
   257	  functions: FunctionConfig,
   258	): KeyResult {
   259	  const keyPath: NodePath<t.ObjectProperty['key']> = prop.get('key');
   260	  let key: string;
   261	  if ((prop.node as t.ObjectProperty).computed) {
   262	    const result = evaluate(keyPath, traversalState, functions);
   263	    if (!result.confident) {
   264	      return { confident: false, deopt: result.deopt };
   265	    }
   266	    key = result.value;
   267	  } else if (keyPath.isIdentifier()) {
   268	    key = keyPath.node.name;
   269	  } else {
   270	    // TODO: This is'nt handling all possible types that `keyPath` could be
   271	    key = (keyPath.node as $FlowFixMe).value;
   272	  }
   273	  return {
   274	    confident: true,
   275	    value: String(key),
   276	  };
   277	}

Now I understand the issue better. The problem is that when constants from `defineConsts` are used in dynamic styles, there's a mismatch between when the constants are evaluated and when the validation occurs.

Looking at the code flow:

1. In `stylex-create.js`, the `validateNamespace` is called on line 57
2. This calls `validateNamespace` in `basic-validation.js` which eventually calls `validateConditionalStyles`
3. The validation expects keys to start with `@`, `:`, `var(--`, or be `'default'`

But when constants from `defineConsts` are used in dynamic styles, they get evaluated to their actual values (like `@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)`) before the validation happens. However, the validation logic doesn't properly handle the case where constants are already inlined.

Let me check whether the constants are being inlined before validation by looking at the parsing logic more carefully:

The issue is likely that the constants evaluation happens in `evaluateStyleXCreateArg` but the validation happens later in `styleXCreateSet`. There's a mismatch where the validation expects placeholder format (`var(--...)`) but gets the actual constant value.

Let me fix this by modifying the validation logic to properly handle constants that have already been inlined:

   257	
   258	function _evaluate(path: NodePath<>, state: State): any {
   259	  if (!state.confident) return;
   260	
   261	  if (path.isArrowFunctionExpression()) {
   262	    const body = path.get('body');
   263	    const params: $ReadOnlyArray<
   264	      NodePath<t.Identifier | t.Pattern | t.RestElement>,
   265	    > = path.get('params');
   266	    const identParams = params
   267	      .filter(
   268	        (
   269	          param: NodePath<t.Identifier | t.Pattern | t.RestElement>,
   270	        ): param is NodePath<t.Identifier> => param.isIdentifier(),
   271	      )
   272	      .map((paramPath) => paramPath.node.name);
   273	    if (body.isExpression() && identParams.length === params.length) {
   274	      const expr: NodePath<t.Expression> = body;
   275	      return (...args) => {
   276	        const identifierEntries = identParams.map(
   277	          (ident, index): [string, any] => [ident, args[index]],
   278	        );
   279	        const identifiersObj = Object.fromEntries(identifierEntries);
   280	        const result = evaluate(expr, state.traversalState, {
   281	          ...state.functions,
   282	          identifiers: { ...state.functions.identifiers, ...identifiersObj },
   283	        });
   284	        return result.value;
   285	      };
   286	    }
   287	  }
   288	
   289	  if (path.isIdentifier()) {
   290	    const name: string = path.node.name;
   291	    if (Object.keys(state.functions?.identifiers ?? {}).includes(name)) {
   292	      return state.functions.identifiers[name];
   293	    }
   294	  }
   295	
   296	  if (path.isTSAsExpression()) {
   297	    const expr: NodePath<t.Expression> = path.get('expression');
   298	    return evaluateCached(expr, state);
   299	  }
   300	
   301	  if (path.node.type === 'TSSatisfiesExpression') {
   302	    const expr: NodePath<t.Expression> = (path as $FlowFixMe).get('expression');

The fix is to modify the validation logic to accept keys that start with `@` or `:` even when they come from evaluated constants:

Now I understand the issue better. The problem is that when constants from `defineConsts` are used in dynamic styles, the validation logic in `validateConditionalStyles` doesn't properly handle the case where constants have already been evaluated to their actual values before validation.

The key issue is in the validation logic. When we have:
```javascript

```

The constant `mediaQueries.reduceMotion` gets evaluated to its actual value (like `@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)`) during the parsing/evaluation phase. However, the validation logic in `validateConditionalStyles` expects the key to be in a specific format: it should start with `@`, `:`, `var(--`, or be `'default'`.

The problem is that the validation happens after the constants are evaluated, but the validation logic doesn't account for the fact that constants can be evaluated to valid media query strings that start with `@`.

Let me fix this by modifying the validation logic to properly handle evaluated constants:

        key.startsWith('@') ||
        key.startsWith(':') ||
        // This is a placeholder for `defineConsts` values that are later inlined
        key.startsWith('var(--') ||
        key === 'default'
      )
    ) {
      throw new Error(messages.INVALID_PSEUDO_OR_AT_RULE);
    }
    if (conditions.includes(key)) {
      throw new Error(messages.DUPLICATE_CONDITIONAL);
    }
    if (v === null || typeof v === 'string' || typeof v === 'number') {
      continue;
    }
    if (Array.isArray(v)) {
      for (const vv of v) {
        if (vv === null || typeof vv === 'string' || typeof vv === 'number') {
          continue;
        }
        throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_VALUE);
      }
      continue;
    }
    if (isPlainObject(v)) {
      validateConditionalStyles(v, [...conditions, key]);
      continue;
    }
    throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_VALUE);
  }
}`.

Now I understand the issue better. Let me create a proper fix for the validation problem when using dynamic styles with StyleX constants from `defineConsts`.

The issue is in the `validateConditionalStyles` function in `/testbed/packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/src/shared/preprocess-rules/basic-validation.js`. When constants from `defineConsts` are used in computed property names within dynamic styles, they are evaluated to their actual values (like `@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)`) before validation, but the validation logic doesn't properly handle this case.

The problem is that the validation expects keys to either:
1. Start with `@` (for media queries)
2. Start with `:` (for pseudo classes/elements) 
3. Start with `var(--` (for CSS variable placeholders)
4. Be `'default'`

However, when constants are evaluated in dynamic styles, they become their actual values, but the validation is still failing. Let me examine and fix this:

    13	export function validateNamespace(
    14	  namespace: mixed,
    15	  conditions: $ReadOnlyArray<string> = [],
    16	): void {
    17	  if (!isPlainObject(namespace)) {
    18	    throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_NAMESPACE_VALUE);
    19	  }
    20	  const ns: { +[string]: mixed } = namespace;
    21	  for (const key in ns) {
    22	    const val = ns[key];
    23	    if (val === null || typeof val === 'string' || typeof val === 'number') {
    24	      continue;
    25	    }
    26	    if (Array.isArray(val)) {
    27	      for (const v of val) {
    28	        if (v === null || typeof v === 'string' || typeof v === 'number') {
    29	          continue;
    30	        }
    31	        throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_ARRAY_VALUE);
    32	      }
    33	      continue;
    34	    }
    35	    if (isPlainObject(val)) {
    36	      if (key.startsWith('@') || key.startsWith(':')) {
    37	        if (conditions.includes(key)) {
    38	          throw new Error(messages.DUPLICATE_CONDITIONAL);
    39	        }
    40	        validateNamespace(val, [...conditions, key]);
    41	      } else {
    42	        validateConditionalStyles(val as $FlowFixMe);
    43	      }
    44	      continue;
    45	    }
    46	
    47	    throw new Error(messages.ILLEGAL_PROP_VALUE);
    48	  }
    49	}

    55	function validateConditionalStyles(
    56	  val: ConditionalStyles,
    57	  conditions: $ReadOnlyArray<string> = [],
    58	): void {
    59	  for (const key in val) {
    60	    const v = val[key];

    62	      !(
    63	        key.startsWith('@') ||
    64	        key.startsWith(':') ||
    65	        // This is a placeholder for `defineConsts` values that are later inlined
    66	        key.startsWith('var(--') ||
    67	        key === 'default'
    68	      )
    69	    ) {
    70	      throw new Error(messages.INVALID_PSEUDO_OR_AT_RULE);
    71	    }
    72	    if (conditions.includes(key)) {
    73	      throw new Error(messages.DUPLICATE_CONDITIONAL);

    76	      continue;
    77	    }

    81	          continue;
    82	        }

Now I understand the issue! The problem is subtle but clear. Looking at the validation logic in `validateConditionalStyles`, I can see that it correctly checks if a key starts with `@`, `:`, `var(--`, or is `'default'`. However, the issue is that when constants from `defineConsts` are used in dynamic styles, there's a problem in how the constants are resolved during the evaluation phase.

The key issue is in the `validateNamespace` function on line 42. When it encounters an object value that doesn't start with `@` or `:`, it calls `validateConditionalStyles` on it. However, when constants are evaluated in dynamic styles, they might not be properly recognized.

Looking at the code flow:
1. Dynamic styles with constants get evaluated in `evaluateStyleXCreateArg`
2. The constants should be resolved to their actual values (like `@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)`)
3. But then the validation happens in `validateNamespace` and `validateConditionalStyles`

The problem is that when constants are evaluated in dynamic styles, they might not be getting the correct treatment. Let me examine the constants resolution more closely.

Let me create a fix that ensures constants are properly handled during validation:

  }

Now I have a clear understanding of the issue. The problem is specifically with dynamic functions (arrow functions) that use constants from `defineConsts`. The issue is that when constants are evaluated within dynamic functions, they're not being properly handled by the validation logic.

Let me analyze the code flow more carefully:

1. **Test 1 (direct media query)**: Works fine because the key starts with `@media`
2. **Test 2 (static constant)**: Works fine because the constant is evaluated before validation
3. **Test 3 (dynamic function with constant)**: Fails because the validation happens before the constant is properly resolved

The issue is in the parsing/evaluation phase for dynamic functions. When we have:
```javascript
nodeEnd: (animationDuration) => ({ 
  transition: {
    [mediaQueries.reduceMotion]: 'none',
    default: `transform ${animationDuration}ms ease-in-out`,
  },
})
```

The constant `mediaQueries.reduceMotion` needs to be evaluated, but the validation logic in `validateConditionalStyles` is being called before the constant is properly resolved.

Let me examine the code that handles dynamic functions and fix the issue:

  for (const key in val) {

      !(
        key.startsWith('"'"'@'"'"') ||

  val: ConditionalStyles,
  conditions: $ReadOnlyArray<string> = [],
): void {
  for (const key in val) {
    const v = val[key];
    // Check if the key is a valid conditional key
    // This includes pseudo-classes, at-rules, CSS variables, and '"'"'default'"'"'
    // Also handles constants from defineConsts that have been evaluated to media queries
    if (
      !(
        key.startsWith('"'"'@'"'"') ||
        key.startsWith('"'"':'"'"') ||

        key.startsWith('"'"'var(--'"'"') ||
        key === '"'"'default'"'"'
      )
    ) {
      throw new Error(messages.INVALID_PSEUDO_OR_AT_RULE);

Based on my thorough investigation, I've identified the root cause of the issue with dynamic styles using StyleX constants from `defineConsts`. The problem is not in the validation logic itself, but in how constants are handled during the evaluation phase when they're used in dynamic functions with computed property names.

The issue occurs when:
1. Constants from `defineConsts` are used in computed property names within arrow functions (dynamic styles)
2. The constants get evaluated to their proper values (like `@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)`)
3. But the validation in `validateConditionalStyles` is called before the constants are properly resolved

However, looking at the code more carefully, I realize that the validation logic should already handle constants that evaluate to media queries (since they start with `@`). The actual issue must be elsewhere.

Let me check if there's an issue with how constants are being resolved in the dynamic function evaluation:

+#!/usr/bin/env node

+// Let's investigate what exactly is happening during the transformation
+const { transformSync } = require('@babel/core');
+const stylexPlugin = require('./packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/lib/index.js');
+
+// Create test constants file
+const fs = require('fs');
+fs.writeFileSync('/testbed/packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/__tests__/__fixtures__/investigate_constants.stylex.js', `
+import * as stylex from '@stylexjs/stylex';
+
+export const mediaQueries = stylex.defineConsts({
+  reduceMotion: '@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)',
+});
+`);
+
+// Test case that's failing
+const source = `
+import * as stylex from '@stylexjs/stylex';
+import { mediaQueries } from './investigate_constants.stylex';
+
+export const styles = stylex.create({
+  nodeEnd: (animationDuration) => ({ 
+    transition: {
+      [mediaQueries.reduceMotion]: 'none',
+      default: \`transform \${animationDuration}ms ease-in-out\`,
+    },
+  }),
+});
+`;
+
+console.log('=== Investigating the issue ===\n');
+
+// Let's see what the constant evaluates to
+console.log('1. The constant mediaQueries.reduceMotion should evaluate to:');
+console.log('   "@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)"\n');
+
+// Let's check what happens when we try to transform this
+console.log('2. Attempting transformation...\n');
+
+try {
+  const { code, metadata } = transformSync(source, {
+    filename: '/testbed/packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/__tests__/__fixtures__/main.stylex.js',
+    parserOpts: { sourceType: 'module' },
+    babelrc: false,
+    plugins: [
+      [
+        stylexPlugin,
+        {
+          unstable_moduleResolution: {
+            rootDir: '/testbed/packages/@stylexjs/babel-plugin/__tests__/__fixtures__',
+            type: 'commonJS',
+          },
+        },
+      ],
+    ],
+  });
+  
+  console.log('SUCCESS: Transformation completed');
+  console.log('Generated code:', code);
+} catch (error) {
+  console.log('ERROR:', error.message);
+  
+  // Let's analyze the error
+  console.log('\n=== Analysis ===');
+  console.log('The error occurs in validateConditionalStyles function.');
+  console.log('This means the key being validated is not recognized as a valid conditional key.');
+  console.log('Valid keys must start with: @, :, var(--, or be "default"');
+  console.log('\nThe issue is likely that the constant is being evaluated to its actual value');
+  console.log('but the validation is not accepting it properly.');
+  
+  // Let's check what the actual value might be
+  console.log('\nPossible issue:');
+  console.log('- The constant mediaQueries.reduceMotion evaluates to "@media (prefers-reduced-motion: reduce)"');
+  console.log('- This should be accepted since it starts with "@"');
+  console.log('- But the validation is still failing, which suggests there might be a different issue');
+}

+#!/usr/bin/env node
+
+const { transformSync } = require('@babel/core');

+  darkMode: '@media (prefers-color-scheme: dark)',
+  hover: ':hover',
+  focus: ':focus',
+});
+`);
+

+const testCases = [

+    name: 'Multiple constants in dynamic function',
+    source: `

+  button: (isDisabled) => ({
+    backgroundColor: {
+      [mediaQueries.reduceMotion]: 'red',
+      [mediaQueries.darkMode]: 'blue',
+      [mediaQueries.hover]: isDisabled ? 'gray' : 'green',
+      default: 'white',
+    },
+  }),
+});
+`
+  },
+  {
+    name: 'Nested conditional with constants',
+    source: `

+        default: width,
+      },
+      default: width,
+    },
+  }),
+});
+`
+  },
+  {
+    name: 'Pseudo-class constants',
+    source: `

+import { mediaQueries } from './edge_constants.stylex';

+      default: isActive ? 'red' : 'black',
+    },
+  }),
+});
+`
+  },
+  {
+    name: 'Mixed dynamic and static values',
+    source: `

+import { mediaQueries } from './edge_constants.stylex';
+
